# Text Elements
Right after the big bang, electrons and quarks began to form.
After the universe cooled more, the lithium, helium, and hydrogen formed.
After the universe cooled even more, the first stars and galaxies were formed, 
these stars and galaxies formed the rest of the periodic table.  ^z0kq5uLX

Right after the big bang, it was too hot for atoms to exist, however, 
after the universe cooled down, protons and neutrons combined, and 
electrons began to orbit around them. So as the big bang progressed, \
more atoms were created ^RuVy8Y5s

U=k(q1*q2)/r where q = charge of the object, and r is the distance between
charges. As electromagnetic forces cause the atoms to get closer, 
the potential energy gets greater as r decreases. ^MHAM6Fnn

U=k(q1q2)/r the potential energy should skyrocket, as the protons
approach r becomes super small, leading the equation to be huge 
 ^s6wV3cjV
